## Overview

### Vision
TestMesh v1.0 dashboard provides a **dual-mode interface** that serves both technical and non-technical users while maintaining professional grade observability and debugging capabilities.

### Scope for v1.0
- âœ… **Form Mode**: Guided, form-based test creation for non-technical users
- âœ… **Power Mode**: Visual DAG editor + DSL editor for engineers
- âœ… **Execution Dashboard**: Real-time test execution with live logs
- âœ… **Debug Tools**: Step replay, pause/resume, request/response viewers
- âœ… **Reporting**: Trends, analytics, flaky test detection
- âœ… **Admin Console**: RBAC, system health, user management
- âœ… **AI Assistant**: Integrated chat and generation features

### Tech Stack
```
Frontend:
- React 18 + TypeScript
- Next.js 14 (App Router)
- TailwindCSS + Shadcn/ui
- React Flow (DAG visualization)
- Monaco Editor (code editing)
- Recharts / Tremor (charts)
- WebSocket (live updates)
- TanStack Query (data fetching)
- Zustand (state management)

Backend Integration:
- REST API (primary)
- WebSocket (live execution)
- gRPC-web (optional, future)
```

---

## Design Principles

### 1. **Progressive Disclosure**
- Simple by default, powerful when needed
- Hide complexity until user requests it
- Smart defaults everywhere

### 2. **Two-Tier UI**
- **Form Mode**: Wizard-based, guided experience
- **Power Mode**: Visual + code, full control

### 3. **Context-Aware**
- Show relevant actions based on user's current task
- Smart suggestions from AI
- Keyboard shortcuts for power users

### 4. **Real-Time Feedback**
- Immediate validation
- Live preview
- Instant error feedback

### 5. **Unified Design Language**
- Consistent components
- Predictable interactions
- Professional aesthetics

---

- **QuickActionCard**: CTA buttons with icons
- **ExecutionList**: Recent runs with status badges
- **HealthChart**: Trend visualization (Recharts)
- **SystemStatus**: Real-time health indicators

#### API Endpoints
```typescript
GET /api/dashboard
  â†’ { quickStats, recentExecutions, healthMetrics, systemStatus }

GET /api/executions/recent?limit=10
  â†’ Execution[]

GET /api/metrics/health?days=7
  â†’ { passRate, avgDuration, flakyTests, trend }
```

#### DAG Interactions
- **Click step**: Open properties panel
- **Double-click step**: Open detailed editor modal
- **Drag from edge**: Create connection
- **Shift + Click**: Multi-select
- **Cmd/Ctrl + C/V**: Copy/paste steps
- **Delete**: Remove selected
- **Cmd/Ctrl + Z**: Undo
- **Cmd/Ctrl + Y**: Redo

#### Step Types (Visual Nodes)

```
HTTP Request           Database Query        Kafka Publish
```

#### Monaco Features
- **Syntax highlighting**: YAML
- **Auto-complete**: Actions, fields, variables
- **Inline validation**: Real-time error checking
- **Quick fixes**: Suggest corrections
- **Hover docs**: Show action documentation
- **Go to definition**: Jump to variable source
- **Snippets**: Common patterns
- **Multi-cursor**: Edit multiple places

---

```
â”‚  â˜‘ Stop on first failure                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ’¡ Tip: Failed steps will run with the same context          â”‚
â”‚     from the original execution                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                â”‚
â”‚                          [Cancel]  [Rerun Failed Steps â†’]     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

#### Execution History with Retry

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Execution History: Payment Gateway Test                       â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤

â”‚  â”‚  #   Status   Duration  Started        By        Actionsâ”‚â”‚
â”‚  â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤â”‚â”‚
```

## Component Library

### Core Components (Shadcn/ui + Custom)

```typescript
// Layout Components
<AppShell>           // Main application layout
<Sidebar>            // Collapsible navigation
<TopBar>             // App header with search/user
<MainContent>        // Content area with padding

// Navigation
<NavItem>            // Sidebar navigation item
<Breadcrumb>         // Breadcrumb navigation
<Tabs>               // Tab navigation

// Form Components
<Input>              // Text input
<Select>             // Dropdown select
<Textarea>           // Multi-line text
<Checkbox>           // Checkbox
<RadioGroup>         // Radio button group
<Switch>             // Toggle switch
<Button>             // Primary/secondary buttons
<IconButton>         // Icon-only button

// Data Display
<Table>              // Data table with sorting/filtering
<Card>               // Content card
<Badge>              // Status badge (âœ… âŒ â±ï¸)
<Tag>                // Label tag
<Avatar>             // User avatar
<Tooltip>            // Hover tooltip
<Popover>            // Click popover

// Feedback
<Alert>              // Alert message
<Toast>              // Notification toast
<Progress>           // Progress bar
<Spinner>            // Loading spinner
<Skeleton>           // Loading placeholder

// Overlays
<Modal>              // Modal dialog
<Drawer>             // Slide-out panel
<Sheet>              // Side sheet

// Data Visualization
<Chart>              // Recharts wrapper
<Timeline>           // Execution timeline
<Waterfall>          // Waterfall chart

// Code Editing

// Flow/DAG

```

## User Flows

### Flow 1: Create Test (Non-Technical User)

```
1. User clicks "New Flow"
2. Mode selector defaults to "Form Mode"
3. Step 1: Enter basic info
   - Name, description, tags
   - Environment variables (guided)
4. Step 2: Add steps (wizard)
   - Click "+ Add Step"
   - Select action type from dropdown
   - Fill form-based configuration
   - See live preview
5. Step 3: Review and test
   - See flow summary
   - Click "Test Run" (dry-run)
6. Step 4: Save
   - Flow saved to "My Flows"
   - Can schedule or run immediately
```

**Time: ~5 minutes** (vs 30+ minutes coding)

### Flow 2: Debug Failed Test (QA Engineer)

```
1. See failed execution in dashboard
2. Click execution â†’ opens Execution View
3. See timeline shows Step 3 failed
4. Click step â†’ Request/Response viewer opens
5. Notice response status 500
6. Click "ğŸ› Debug"
7. Debug panel opens:
   - Set breakpoint at Step 3
   - Override variable: use different API key
   - Click "Replay from Step 2"
8. Step runs, pauses at breakpoint
9. Edit payload in debug panel
10. Click "Continue"
11. Test passes!
12. Save corrected variable to flow
```

**Time: ~3 minutes** (vs 20+ minutes traditional debugging)

### Flow 3: Generate Test with AI (Backend Dev)

```
1. Click "ğŸ¤– AI Generate"
2. AI chat opens
3. User types: "Test user registration API"
4. AI asks clarifying questions:
   - HTTP or gRPC?
   - Mock database?
   - What assertions?
5. User answers via buttons or text
6. AI generates flow in ~10 seconds
7. User reviews in DAG mode
8. Makes minor edits
9. Runs test â†’ passes!
10. Saves to repository
```

**Time: ~2 minutes** (vs 1+ hour manual creation)

### Flow 4: Monitor System Health (SRE)

```
1. SRE opens Admin Console
2. Dashboard shows:
   - 5/5 workers healthy âœ…
   - 0 jobs in queue âœ…
   - Database latency 45ms âœ…
3. Notice P95 latency spike in chart
4. Click "Workers" tab
5. See worker-4 CPU at 85%
6. Click worker-4 â†’ drill-down
7. See 3 long-running executions
8. Click execution â†’ identify slow SQL query
9. Optimize query or add index
10. Monitor shows improvement
```

**Time: ~5 minutes** (identified and resolved)

### Flow 5: Collaborate on Flow (Team Lead)

```
1. Team lead opens flow in DAG mode
2. Makes changes to Step 3
3. Adds comment on Step 3:
   "@sarah Can you review this timeout change?"
4. Sarah gets notification
5. Sarah opens flow, sees highlighted node
6. Clicks comment â†’ thread opens
7. Adds reply: "LGTM! âœ…"
8. Team lead clicks "Request Review"
9. Selects Sarah and Bob as reviewers
10. Both approve via approval modal
11. Team lead clicks "Publish"
12. Flow v1.6 goes live
```

**Time: ~8 minutes** (collaborative review)

### Flow 6: Rollback to Previous Version (DevOps)

```
1. Production flow failing after latest deploy
2. DevOps opens flow â†’ clicks "History"
3. See v1.8 (current) is broken
4. Click "Compare" to see diff from v1.7
5. Notice problematic timeout change
6. Click "Restore v1.7"
7. Confirmation modal appears
8. Add note: "Rollback: timeout too aggressive"
9. Click "Restore and Publish"
10. v1.7 restored as v1.9 (new version)
11. Tests pass again! âœ…
```

**Time: ~2 minutes** (fast rollback)

### Flow 7: Schedule Event-Based Test (Platform Engineer)

```
1. Click "+ New Schedule"
2. Select trigger type: "Event-Based"
3. Configure:
   - Source: Kafka
   - Topic: "order.created"
   - Filter: $.amount > 100
   - Rate limit: 10 per minute
4. Select flow: "validate-order-test"
5. Enable "Pass event data to flow"
6. Click "Test Trigger" â†’ sees sample event
7. Click "Save & Enable"
8. Schedule now active
9. Production order created â†’ test runs automatically
10. See execution in real-time
```

**Time: ~4 minutes** (automated testing)

### Flow 8: Debug Production Issue (SRE)

```
1. Alert: K8s worker-3 pod crashed
2. Open Infrastructure View
3. See worker-3 with âš ï¸ warning
4. Click worker-3 â†’ Pod Details opens
5. See "3 restarts in last 10 minutes"
6. Click "View Logs"
7. Log viewer shows OOM error
8. Click "Resource Charts" tab
9. See memory spike before crash
10. Click "Scale Up" â†’ increase memory limit
11. Pod restarts with more memory
12. Tests run successfully
```

**Time: ~3 minutes** (diagnosed and fixed)

### Flow 9: Extend Platform with Plugin (Developer)

```
1. Click "Plugins" in sidebar
2. Search "Datadog"
3. Find "Datadog Integration" plugin
4. Click plugin card â†’ see details
5. Read description and reviews (4.8â˜…)
6. Click "Install"
7. Select version: "v2.1.0 (latest)"
8. Click "Confirm Install"
9. Plugin installed â†’ "Configure" button appears
10. Click "Configure"
11. Enter API key and region
12. Click "Test Connection" â†’ âœ… Success
13. Save configuration
14. Now can use Datadog actions in flows
```

**Time: ~3 minutes** (extended capabilities)

### Flow 10: Onboard New Team Member (New User)

```
1. First login â†’ Welcome wizard appears
2. Step 1: Choose role (QA Engineer)
3. Step 2: Quick tour of UI
   - Shows dashboard, flow builder, execution view
4. Step 3: Interactive tutorial
   - Create first flow (guided)
   - Add 3 steps (HTTP â†’ Assert â†’ Log)
   - Run test
5. Step 4: Browse sample flows
   - User imports "API Testing 101"
6. Step 5: Set up first schedule
   - Cron: daily at 9am
7. Wizard complete! ğŸ‰
8. User is productive immediately
```

**Time: ~10 minutes** (complete onboarding)

## API Contracts

### REST API Endpoints (v1.0)

```typescript
// ============================================================================
// Flows
// ============================================================================

GET /api/flows
  â†’ { flows: Flow[], total: number }

GET /api/flows/:id
  â†’ Flow

POST /api/flows
  body: CreateFlowRequest
  â†’ { flow: Flow }

PUT /api/flows/:id
  body: UpdateFlowRequest
  â†’ { flow: Flow }

DELETE /api/flows/:id
  â†’ { success: boolean }

POST /api/flows/:id/validate
  â†’ { valid: boolean, errors: ValidationError[] }

// ============================================================================
// Executions
// ============================================================================

POST /api/executions
  body: { flowId: string, env: string, variables: object }
  â†’ { execution: Execution }

GET /api/executions/:id
  â†’ Execution

GET /api/executions/:id/steps
  â†’ { steps: StepExecution[] }

GET /api/executions/:id/logs
  â†’ { logs: LogEntry[] }

POST /api/executions/:id/pause
  â†’ { success: boolean }

POST /api/executions/:id/resume
  â†’ { success: boolean }

POST /api/executions/:id/stop
  â†’ { success: boolean }

POST /api/executions/:id/replay
  body: { fromStep: string }
  â†’ { execution: Execution }

// ============================================================================
// AI
// ============================================================================

POST /api/ai/generate
  body: { description: string, context: object }
  â†’ { flow: Flow, files: GeneratedFile[] }

POST /api/ai/chat
  body: { message: string, conversationId?: string }
  â†’ { response: string, conversationId: string }

POST /api/ai/analyze-failure
  body: { executionId: string, stepId: string }
  â†’ { analysis: FailureAnalysis, suggestions: Fix[] }

POST /api/ai/import
  body: { source: 'openapi'|'pact'|'postman', file: File }
  â†’ { flows: Flow[] }

// ============================================================================
// Reports
// ============================================================================

GET /api/reports/dashboard
  query: { days: number }
  â†’ { stats: DashboardStats }

GET /api/reports/trends
  query: { days: number }
  â†’ { trends: TrendData[] }

GET /api/reports/flaky
  â†’ { flakyTests: FlakyTest[] }

GET /api/reports/coverage
  â†’ { coverage: CoverageData }

// ============================================================================
// Admin
// ============================================================================

GET /api/admin/health
  â†’ { status: SystemHealth }

GET /api/admin/workers
  â†’ { workers: Worker[] }

GET /api/admin/queue
  â†’ { queues: QueueStatus[] }

GET /api/admin/users
  â†’ { users: User[] }

POST /api/admin/users
  body: CreateUserRequest
  â†’ { user: User }

PUT /api/admin/users/:id/role
  body: { role: string }
  â†’ { user: User }

GET /api/admin/audit
  query: { from: date, to: date, user?: string }
  â†’ { events: AuditEvent[] }

// ============================================================================
// Version Control
// ============================================================================

GET /api/flows/:id/versions
  query: { limit: number, offset: number }
  â†’ { versions: FlowVersion[], total: number }

GET /api/flows/:id/versions/:versionId
  â†’ FlowVersion

POST /api/flows/:id/versions/:versionId/restore
  â†’ { flow: Flow }

POST /api/flows/:id/publish
  body: { notes?: string, scheduleAt?: date }
  â†’ { flow: Flow, version: FlowVersion }

POST /api/flows/:id/draft
  â†’ { flow: Flow }

DELETE /api/flows/:id/draft
  â†’ { success: boolean }

GET /api/flows/:id/versions/compare
  query: { from: string, to: string }
  â†’ { diff: DiffData }

// ============================================================================
// Comments & Collaboration
// ============================================================================

GET /api/flows/:id/comments
  â†’ { comments: Comment[] }

  body: { content: string }
  â†’ { comment: Comment }

  â†’ { success: boolean }

  body: { content: string, mentions: string[] }
  â†’ { comment: Comment }

  body: { type: 'ğŸ‘'|'ğŸ‘'|'âœ…' }
  â†’ { success: boolean }

  â†’ { success: boolean }
```

### WebSocket Events

```typescript
// Connect
ws://localhost:3000/ws/executions/:executionId

// Events sent from server
{
  "event": "execution.started",
  "data": { executionId: string, startedAt: string }
}

{
  "event": "step.started",
  "data": { stepId: string, stepName: string }
}

{
  "event": "step.completed",
  "data": { stepId: string, duration: number, status: string }
}

{
  "event": "log",
  "data": { level: string, message: string, timestamp: string }
}

{
  "event": "execution.completed",
  "data": { executionId: string, status: string, duration: number }
}

// Events sent from client
{
  "action": "pause"
}

{
  "action": "resume"
}

{
  "action": "stop"
}
```

### TypeScript Types

```typescript
interface Flow {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description?: string;
  tags: string[];
  env: Record<string, string>;
  steps: Step[];
  setup?: Step[];
  teardown?: Step[];
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
  createdBy: string;
}

interface Step {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  action: ActionType;
  config: Record<string, any>;
  output?: Record<string, string>;
  assert?: Assertion[];
  when?: string;
  onError?: 'continue' | 'fail';
  retry?: RetryConfig;
}

type ActionType =
  | 'http_request'
  | 'database_query'
  | 'kafka_publish'
  | 'kafka_consume'
  | 'assert'
  | 'delay'
  | 'transform'
  | 'for_each'
  | 'run_flow'
  | 'mock_server_start';

interface Execution {
  id: string;
  flowId: string;
  status: 'pending' | 'running' | 'paused' | 'completed' | 'failed';
  startedAt: string;
  completedAt?: string;
  duration?: number;
  env: string;
  variables: Record<string, any>;
  steps: StepExecution[];
}

interface StepExecution {
  id: string;
  stepId: string;
  status: 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'skipped';
  startedAt?: string;
  completedAt?: string;
  duration?: number;
  input?: any;
  output?: any;
  error?: string;
}

interface FailureAnalysis {
  rootCause: string;
  failureType: 'assertion' | 'timeout' | 'network' | 'data' | 'logic';
  confidence: number;
  evidence: string[];
}

interface Fix {
  description: string;
  changes: CodeChange[];
  confidence: number;
}

interface SystemHealth {
  status: 'healthy' | 'degraded' | 'unhealthy';
  workers: WorkerHealth[];
  database: { status: string; latency: number };
  redis: { status: string; latency: number };
  queue: { depth: number };
}
```

---

## Responsive Design

### Breakpoints

```typescript
const breakpoints = {
  mobile: '< 768px',
  tablet: '768px - 1024px',
  desktop: '> 1024px',
  wide: '> 1440px'
};
```

### Layout Adaptations

#### Desktop (> 1024px)
- Full sidebar navigation
- Multi-column layouts
- DAG canvas with properties panel
- Side-by-side request/response viewers

#### Tablet (768px - 1024px)
- Collapsible sidebar
- Single column with tabs
- Simplified DAG (mobile coming with swipe up for detail)
- Stacked request/response

#### Mobile (< 768px)
- Bottom navigation bar
- Full-screen modals
- Form mode only (no DAG)
- Accordion-style lists
- Simplified execution view

### Mobile-First Components

```tsx
// Responsive container
<Container className="px-4 md:px-6 lg:px-8">

// Responsive grid
<Grid className="grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3">

// Responsive text
<Text className="text-sm md:text-base lg:text-lg">

// Hide on mobile
<div className="hidden md:block">

// Show only on mobile
<div className="block md:hidden">
```

---

## Accessibility

### WCAG 2.1 AA Compliance

#### Keyboard Navigation
- âœ… All actions accessible via keyboard
- âœ… Visible focus indicators
- âœ… Logical tab order
- âœ… Keyboard shortcuts with visual hints
- âœ… Escape to close modals

#### Screen Readers
- âœ… Semantic HTML (nav, main, aside, article)
- âœ… ARIA labels on all interactive elements
- âœ… ARIA live regions for dynamic content
- âœ… Alt text on all images/icons
- âœ… Descriptive link text

#### Visual
- âœ… Minimum contrast ratio 4.5:1
- âœ… Resizable text (up to 200%)
- âœ… No information by color alone
- âœ… Clear error messages
- âœ… Loading states

#### Example
```tsx
<Button
  onClick={handleSave}
  aria-label="Save flow"
  disabled={!isDirty}
>
  <SaveIcon aria-hidden="true" />
  <span>Save</span>
</Button>

<Input
  type="text"
  id="flow-name"
  aria-describedby="flow-name-hint"
  aria-required="true"
  aria-invalid={errors.name ? "true" : "false"}
/>
<span id="flow-name-hint" className="text-sm text-gray-600">
  Enter a descriptive name for your test flow
</span>
{errors.name && (
  <span role="alert" className="text-red-600">
    {errors.name.message}
  </span>
)}
```

**âœ… All P1 High Priority Features** (100% coverage):

**âœ… All P2 Medium Priority Features** (100% coverage):
- Plugin marketplace (browse, install, configure)
